SUMMARY OF CASUALTIES

SUMMARY OF ALL CASUALTIES
IN THEIR RESPECTIVE UNITS
Up to and including 14th August, 1917.
WELLINGTON
MY AUTHORITY : MARCUS F. MARKS, GOVERNMENT PRINTER.
